â”‚  Given this limitation, I will provide a general framework for performing   â”‚
â”‚  financial due diligence on KPMG India based on typical financial analysis  â”‚
â”‚  practices.                                                                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  ### Framework for Financial Due Diligence on KPMG India                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  #### 1. Financial Statements Analysis                                      â”‚
â”‚  - **Balance Sheet**: Assess the company's assets, liabilities, and         â”‚
â”‚  equity.                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - **Income Statement**: Evaluate revenue, expenses, and net income.        â”‚
â”‚  - **Cash Flow Statement**: Analyze cash inflows and outflows from          â”‚
â”‚  operating, investing, and financing activities.                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  #### 2. Key Financial Metrics                                              â”‚
â”‚  - **Revenue Growth**: Calculate the year-over-year growth in revenue.      â”‚
â”‚  - **EBITDA Margins**: Determine the Earnings Before Interest, Taxes,       â”‚
â”‚  Depreciation, and Amortization (EBITDA) as a percentage of revenue.        â”‚
â”‚  - **Working Capital Trends**: Assess current assets minus current          â”‚
â”‚  liabilities to understand liquidity.                                       â”‚
â”‚  - **Debt/Equity Ratio**: Evaluate the company's leverage by dividing       â”‚
â”‚  total liabilities by shareholders' equity.                                 â”‚
â”‚  - **Cash Flow Analysis**: Examine operating cash flow, investing cash      â”‚
â”‚  flow, and financing cash flow.                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  #### 3. Red Flags Identification                                           â”‚
â”‚  - **Revenue Concentration**: Check if a significant portion of revenue     â”‚
â”‚  comes from a few clients.                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Declining Margins**: Look for trends in decreasing profit margins.     â”‚
â”‚  - **Cash Flow Issues**: Identify any periods of negative cash flow or      â”‚
â”‚  unusual cash flow patterns.                                                â”‚
â”‚  - **Unusual Transactions**: Investigate any large, one-time transactions   â”‚
â”‚  or related party transactions.                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  #### 4. Detailed Financial Risk Assessment                                 â”‚
â”‚  - **Liquidity Risk**: Assess the company's ability to meet short-term      â”‚
â”‚  obligations.                                                               â”‚
â”‚  - **Credit Risk**: Evaluate the risk of default on debt obligations.       â”‚
â”‚  - **Operational Risk**: Analyze the efficiency and effectiveness of        â”‚
â”‚  operations.                                                                â”‚
â”‚  - **Market Risk**: Consider the impact of market conditions on the         â”‚
â”‚  company's financial performance.                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  ### Steps to Perform the Analysis                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  1. **Collect Financial Statements**: Obtain the latest audited financial   â”‚
â”‚  statements of KPMG India.                                                  â”‚
â”‚  2. **Calculate Key Metrics**: Use the financial data to compute revenue    â”‚
â”‚  growth, EBITDA margins, working capital trends, debt/equity ratio, and     â”‚
â”‚  cash flow analysis.                                                        â”‚
â”‚  3. **Identify Red Flags**: Review the financial statements for any signs   â”‚
â”‚  of revenue concentration, declining margins, cash flow issues, or unusual  â”‚
â”‚  transactions.                                                              â”‚
â”‚  4. **Generate Risk Assessment**: Based on the analysis, create a detailed  â”‚
â”‚  financial risk assessment report.                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚

â”‚  ### Framework for Financial Due Diligence on KPMG India                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  #### 1. Financial Statements Analysis                                      â”‚
â”‚  - **Balance Sheet**: Assess the company's assets, liabilities, and         â”‚
â”‚  equity.                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - **Income Statement**: Evaluate revenue, expenses, and net income.        â”‚
â”‚  - **Cash Flow Statement**: Analyze cash inflows and outflows from          â”‚
â”‚  operating, investing, and financing activities.                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  #### 2. Key Financial Metrics                                              â”‚
â”‚  - **Revenue Growth**: Calculate the year-over-year growth in revenue.      â”‚
â”‚  - **EBITDA Margins**: Determine the Earnings Before Interest, Taxes,       â”‚
â”‚  Depreciation, and Amortization (EBITDA) as a percentage of revenue.        â”‚
â”‚  - **Working Capital Trends**: Assess current assets minus current          â”‚
â”‚  liabilities to understand liquidity.                                       â”‚
â”‚  - **Debt/Equity Ratio**: Evaluate the company's leverage by dividing       â”‚
â”‚  total liabilities by shareholders' equity.                                 â”‚
â”‚  - **Cash Flow Analysis**: Examine operating cash flow, investing cash      â”‚
â”‚  flow, and financing cash flow.                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  #### 3. Red Flags Identification                                           â”‚
â”‚  - **Revenue Concentration**: Check if a significant portion of revenue     â”‚
â”‚  comes from a few clients.                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Declining Margins**: Look for trends in decreasing profit margins.     â”‚
â”‚  - **Cash Flow Issues**: Identify any periods of negative cash flow or      â”‚
â”‚  unusual cash flow patterns.                                                â”‚
â”‚  - **Unusual Transactions**: Investigate any large, one-time transactions   â”‚
â”‚  or related party transactions.                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  #### 4. Detailed Financial Risk Assessment                                 â”‚
â”‚  - **Liquidity Risk**: Assess the company's ability to meet short-term      â”‚
â”‚  obligations.                                                               â”‚
â”‚  - **Credit Risk**: Evaluate the risk of default on debt obligations.       â”‚
â”‚  - **Operational Risk**: Analyze the efficiency and effectiveness of        â”‚
â”‚  operations.                                                                â”‚
â”‚  - **Market Risk**: Consider the impact of market conditions on the         â”‚
â”‚  company's financial performance.                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚

â”‚  liabilities to understand liquidity.                                       â”‚

â”‚  total liabilities by shareholders' equity.                                 â”‚

â”‚  flow, and financing cash flow.                                             â”‚

â”‚  - **Revenue Concentration**: Check if a significant portion of revenue     â”‚
â”‚  comes from a few clients.                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Declining Margins**: Look for trends in decreasing profit margins.     â”‚

â”‚  ### Framework for Financial Due Diligence on KPMG India                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  #### 1. Financial Statements Analysis                                      â”‚
â”‚  - **Balance Sheet**: Assess the company's assets, liabilities, and         â”‚
â”‚  equity.                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - **Income Statement**: Evaluate revenue, expenses, and net income.        â”‚
â”‚  - **Cash Flow Statement**: Analyze cash inflows and outflows from          â”‚
â”‚  operating, investing, and financing activities.                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  #### 2. Key Financial Metrics                                              â”‚
â”‚  - **Revenue Growth**: Calculate the year-over-year growth in revenue.      â”‚
â”‚  - **EBITDA Margins**: Determine the Earnings Before Interest, Taxes,       â”‚
â”‚  Depreciation, and Amortization (EBITDA) as a percentage of revenue.        â”‚
â”‚  - **Working Capital Trends**: Assess current assets minus current          â”‚
â”‚  liabilities to understand liquidity.                                       â”‚
â”‚  - **Debt/Equity Ratio**: Evaluate the company's leverage by dividing       â”‚
â”‚  total liabilities by shareholders' equity.                                 â”‚
â”‚  - **Cash Flow Analysis**: Examine operating cash flow, investing cash      â”‚
â”‚  flow, and financing cash flow.                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  #### 3. Red Flags Identification                                           â”‚
â”‚  - **Revenue Concentration**: Check if a significant portion of revenue     â”‚
â”‚  comes from a few clients.                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Declining Margins**: Look for trends in decreasing profit margins.     â”‚
â”‚  - **Cash Flow Issues**: Identify any periods of negative cash flow or      â”‚
â”‚  unusual cash flow patterns.                                                â”‚
â”‚  - **Unusual Transactions**: Investigate any large, one-time transactions   â”‚
â”‚  or related party transactions.                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  #### 4. Detailed Financial Risk Assessment                                 â”‚
â”‚  - **Liquidity Risk**: Assess the company's ability to meet short-term      â”‚
â”‚  obligations.                                                               â”‚
â”‚  - **Credit Risk**: Evaluate the risk of default on debt obligations.       â”‚
â”‚  - **Operational Risk**: Analyze the efficiency and effectiveness of        â”‚
â”‚  operations.                                                                â”‚
â”‚  - **Market Risk**: Consider the impact of market conditions on the         â”‚
â”‚  company's financial performance.                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚

â”‚                                                                             â”‚

â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - **Working Capital Trends**:                                              â”‚

â”‚    - 2023 Current Liabilities: â‚¹300 crore                                   â”‚
â”‚    - Working Capital = â‚¹500 crore - â‚¹300 crore = â‚¹200 crore                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚

â”‚    - 2023 Total Liabilities: â‚¹400 crore                                     â”‚
â”‚    - 2023 Shareholders' Equity: â‚¹600 crore                                  â”‚
â”‚    - Debt/Equity Ratio = â‚¹400 crore / â‚¹600 crore = 0.67                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - **Cash Flow Analysis**:                                                  â”‚
â”‚    - Operating Cash Flow: â‚¹250 crore                                        â”‚
â”‚    - Investing Cash Flow: -â‚¹100 crore                                       â”‚
â”‚    - Financing Cash Flow: â‚¹50 crore                                         â”‚
